+    func listneToRemoteConfig() {
+        remoteConfigScheduler.start(
+configCallBack: { config in
+
+            if let appConfig = AppConfig.from(dictionary: config) {
+                
+                // checking maintenance
+                if appConfig.maintenance.enabled {
+                    DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                        withAnimation {
+                            navigationManager.configTap = .mainMaintenance(model: appConfig.maintenance)
+                        }
+                    }
+                    return
+                } else {
+                    DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                        withAnimation {
+                            navigationManager.configTap = nil
+                        }
+                    }
+                }
+                
+                // checking updates
+                if appConfig.update.hard.enabled || appConfig.update.soft.enabled {
+                    
+                    let isHardUpdate = appConfig.update.hard.enabled
+                    let redirectURL: String = appConfig.update.redirectURL
+                    let updateModel = isHardUpdate ? appConfig.update.hard : appConfig.update.soft
+                    
+                    // Showing soft update only once in the app run cycle
+                    if !isHardUpdate && LocalSettings.softUpdateShown { return }
+                    
+                    
+                    // checking version max min fall
+                    guard let version = Int(Bundle.main.object(forInfoDictionaryKey: "CFBundleShortVersionString") as? String ?? "") else {
+                        return
+                    }
+                    if isHardUpdate {
+                        if let max = Int(appConfig.update.hard.max),
+                           let min = Int(appConfig.update.hard.min) {
+                            if !(max <= version && version >= min) {
+                                return
+                            }
+                        }
+                    } else {
+                        if let max = Int(appConfig.update.soft.max),
+                           let min = Int(appConfig.update.soft.min) {
+                            if !(max <= version && version >= min) {
+                                return
+                            }
+                        }
+                    }
+                    DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                        withAnimation {
+                            navigationManager.configTap =
+                                .update(
+                                    isHardUpdate: isHardUpdate,
+                                    model: updateModel,
+                                    redirectURL: redirectURL
+                                )
+                        }
+                    }
+                } else {
+                    DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                        withAnimation {
+                            navigationManager.configTap = nil
+                        }
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+        })
+    }

+    func clearCoreData() throws {
+        let coordinator = container.persistentStoreCoordinator
+        for store in coordinator.persistentStores {
+            if let url = store.url {
+                try coordinator.destroyPersistentStore(at: url, ofType: store.type, options: nil)
+                try coordinator.addPersistentStore(ofType: store.type, configurationName: nil, at: url, options: nil)
+                LocalSettings.totalAutomation = 0
+            }
+        }
+    }

+    func updateAuthToken(tokenString: String) async throws {
+        
+        if client == nil {
+            debugPrint("Client not connected, calling connect function...")
+            await connect()
+        }
+        guard let greeter = client else {
+            print("Client not connected.")
+            return
+        }
+        
+        print("idToken \(tokenString)")
+
+        let request = GRPCCore.StreamingClientRequest<ComputerUse_Service_AuthToken> { writer in
+            var token = ComputerUse_Service_AuthToken()
+            token.idToken = tokenString
+            token.timestamp = Int64(Date().timeIntervalSince1970)
+
+            try await writer.write(token)
+        }
+
+        let _ = try await greeter.authHandshake(request: request) { response in
+            switch response.accepted {
+            case .success(let contents):
+                for try await part in contents.bodyParts {
+                    if case .message(let msg) = part {
+                        print("Status:", msg)
+                    }
+                }
+            case .failure(let err):
+                throw err
+            }
+
+            return true
+        }
+
+    }
 
 }

diff --git a/app/macos/ComputerUse/Sources/Helper/FirebaseConfig/FirebaseConfigModel.swift b/app/macos/ComputerUse/Sources/Helper/FirebaseConfig/FirebaseConfigModel.swift

+++ b/app/macos/ComputerUse/Sources/Helper/FirebaseConfig/FirebaseConfigModel.swift
@@ -0,0 +1,48 @@
+import Foundation
+
+struct AppConfig: Codable {
+    let maintenance: Maintenance
+    let update: UpdateConfig
+
+    // MARK: - Convert [String: Any]  Model
+    static func from(dictionary: [String: Any?]) -> AppConfig? {
+        do {
+            let data = try JSONSerialization.data(withJSONObject: dictionary, options: [])
+            let decoder = JSONDecoder()
+            return try decoder.decode(AppConfig.self, from: data)
+        } catch {
+            print("Failed to decode AppConfig:", error)
+            return nil
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+struct Maintenance: Codable {
+    let enabled: Bool
+    let title: String
+    let message: String
+    let cta: CTA
+}
+
+struct CTA: Codable {
+    let text: String
+    let redirect: String
+}
+
+struct UpdateConfig: Codable {
+    let soft: UpdateType
+    let hard: UpdateType
+    let redirectURL: String
+    
+    enum CodingKeys: String, CodingKey {
+        case soft, hard
+        case redirectURL = "redirect_url"
+    }
+}
+
+struct UpdateType: Codable {
+    let enabled: Bool
+    let min: String
+    let max: String
+    let message: String
+}

+        let settings = RemoteConfigSettings()
+        settings.minimumFetchInterval = 60
+        remoteConfig.configSettings = settings
+    }
+
+    func start(configCallBack: @escaping (_ config: [String: Any]) -> Void) {
+        fetch(onConfigFetched: configCallBack)
+
+        // Schedule repeated fetch every 10 mins
+        timer = Timer.scheduledTimer(withTimeInterval: 60, repeats: true) { [weak self] _ in
+            self?.fetch(onConfigFetched: configCallBack)
+        }
+        timer?.fire()
+    }
+
+    private func fetch(onConfigFetched: @escaping ([String: Any?]) -> Void) {
+        remoteConfig.fetchAndActivate { status, error in
+            
+            if let dict = self.remoteConfig["REMOTE_CONFIG_PROD"].jsonValue as? [String: Any?] {
+                onConfigFetched(dict)
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+import Foundation
+import SwiftUI
+
+struct SuggestionTaskBoardView: View {
+    @State private var selectedTab: TabType = .suggestions
+    @State private var currentIndex: Int = 0
+    @State private var pinned: [SavedAutomationModel] = []
+    @State private var isPinnedEmpty = false
+    
+    let itemsPerPage = 6
+    @State private var pageIndex = 0
+    @State private var visiblePageID: Int? = 0
+    
+    var totalPages: Int {
+        let count = selectedTab == .suggestions ? suggestions.count : pinned.count
+        return count % itemsPerPage == 0
+            ? count / itemsPerPage
+            : count / itemsPerPage + 1
+    }
+
+    var onSelected: (_ item: TaskItem?, _  automation: SavedAutomationModel?) -> Void
+    
+    private let suggestions: [TaskItem] = TaskItem.getSuggestions()
+    
+    var body: some View {
+        VStack(alignment: .center, spacing: 16) {
+            
+            // Toggle Tabs
+            HStack {
+                HStack(spacing: 12) {
+                    tabButton(.suggestions, label: "Suggestions")
+                    tabButton(.pinned, label: "Pinned")
+                }
+                .cornerRadius(8)
+                
+                Spacer()
+            }
+            .padding(.horizontal, .innerPadding)
+            .frame(width: .innerCardWidth)
+
+            ScrollViewReader { proxy in
+                HStack(alignment: .center) {
+                    
+                    Button(action: {
+                        withAnimation {
+                            if pageIndex > 0 {
+                                pageIndex -= 1
+                                proxy.scrollTo(pageIndex, anchor: .leading)
+                            }
+                        }
+                    }) {
+                        HStack {
+                            Image(systemName: "chevron.left")
+                                .foregroundColor(
+                                    pageIndex > 0 ? Color.icon.tertiary : Color.icon.disabled
+                                )
+                                .font(.body1)
+                        }
+                        .background(Color.background.primary)
+                    }
+                    .buttonStyle(.plain)
+                    .pointerStyle(.link)
+                    .opacity(totalPages > 1 ? 1 : 0)
+                    .allowsHitTesting(totalPages > 1)
+                    
+                    ScrollView(.horizontal) {
+                        HStack(spacing: 0) {
+                            ForEach(0..<totalPages, id: \.self) { page in
+                                gridForPage(page)
+                                    .frame(width: .innerCardWidth)
+                                    .containerRelativeFrame(.horizontal)
+                            }
+                        }
+                        .scrollTargetLayout()
+                    }
+                    .scrollPosition(id: $visiblePageID)
+                    .scrollTargetBehavior(.paging)
+                    .scrollIndicators(.never)
+                    .frame(height: 255)
+                    .onChange(of: visiblePageID) {
+                        if let newID = visiblePageID {
+                            pageIndex = newID
+                        }
+                    }
+                    
+                    Button(action: {
+                        withAnimation {
+                            if pageIndex < totalPages - 1 {
+                                pageIndex += 1
+                                proxy.scrollTo(pageIndex, anchor: .leading)
+                            }
+                        }
+                    }) {
+                        HStack {
+                            Image(systemName: "chevron.right")
+                                .foregroundColor(
+                                    pageIndex < (totalPages - 1) ? Color.icon.tertiary : Color.icon.disabled
+                                )                                .font(.body1)
+                        }
+                        .background(Color.background.primary)
+                    }
+                    .buttonStyle(.plain)
+                    .pointerStyle(.link)
+                    .opacity(totalPages > 1 ? 1 : 0)
+                    .allowsHitTesting(totalPages > 1)
+                }
+                .padding(.horizontal, .innerPadding)
+                
+                HStack(alignment: .center) {
+                    HStack(spacing: 10) {
+                        ForEach(0..<totalPages, id: \.self) { index in
+                            Circle()
+                                .fill(index == pageIndex ? Color.accent.primary : Color.background.secondary)
+                                .frame(width: 8, height: 8)
+                                .pointerStyle(.link)
+                                .hoverPointer(with: Color.background.secondary.opacity(0.5))
+                                .onTapGesture {
+                                    withAnimation {
+                                        proxy.scrollTo(index, anchor: .leading)
+                                        pageIndex = index
+                                    }
+                                }
+                        }
+                    }
+                    .frame(width: 82)
+                }
+                .padding(.top, .cardSeparationPadding)
+                .opacity(totalPages > 1 ? 1 : 0)
+                .allowsHitTesting(totalPages > 1)
+
+            }
+            .scrollIndicators(.hidden)
+
+            
+        }
+        .overlay(content: {
+            if isPinnedEmpty && selectedTab == .pinned {
+                EmptyListView(animationName: "emptyViewLotti.json", title: "No Pinned Automations", subtitle: "You havent pinned any automations yet. Browse your automation list and pin your favourites to access them quickly.")
+                    .frame(maxWidth: 450, maxHeight: .infinity, alignment: .bottom)
+            }
+        })
+        .frame(width: .suggestionCardWidth)
+        .onAppear {
+            Task { fetchPinnedAutomation() }
+        }
+    }
+    
+    @ViewBuilder
+    func suggestionsGrid(_ page: Int) -> some View {
+        let start = page * itemsPerPage
+        let end = min(start + itemsPerPage, suggestions.count)
+        let slice = Array(suggestions[start..<end])
+
+        let columns = [
+            GridItem(.fixed(280), spacing: 14),
+            GridItem(.fixed(280), spacing: 14),
+            GridItem(.fixed(280), spacing: 14)
+        ]
+
+        LazyVGrid(columns: columns, alignment: .center, spacing: 14) {
+            ForEach(slice, id: \.id) { item in
+                TaskCard(item: item)
+                    .onTapGesture { onSelected(item, nil) }
+            }
+        }
+        .frame(maxHeight: .infinity, alignment: .topLeading)
+    }
+
+    @ViewBuilder
+    func pinnedGrid(_ page: Int) -> some View {
+        let start = page * itemsPerPage
+        let end = min(start + itemsPerPage, pinned.count)
+        let slice = Array(pinned[start..<end])
+
+        let columns = [
+            GridItem(.fixed(280), spacing: 14),
+            GridItem(.fixed(280), spacing: 14),
+            GridItem(.fixed(280), spacing: 14)
+        ]
+
+        LazyVGrid(columns: columns, alignment: .center, spacing: 14) {
+            ForEach(slice, id: \.id) { item in
+                TaskCard(automation: item)
+                    .onTapGesture { onSelected(nil, item) }
+            }
+        }
+        .frame(maxHeight: .infinity, alignment: .topLeading)
+    }
+    
+    @ViewBuilder
+    func gridForPage(_ page: Int) -> some View {
+        if selectedTab == .suggestions {
+            suggestionsGrid(page)
+        } else {
+            pinnedGrid(page)
+        }
+    }
+    
+    func fetchPinnedAutomation() {
+        do {
+            pinned = try AutomationStorageManager.shared.fetchPinnedAutomation()
+            print("Pinned count: \(pinned.count)")
+            isPinnedEmpty = pinned.isEmpty
+        } catch {
+            
+        }
+    }
+    
+    // Tab button
+    private func tabButton(_ type: TabType, label: String) -> some View {
+        Button(action: {
+            withAnimation {
+                selectedTab = type
+                pageIndex = 0
+            }
+        }) {
+            VStack {
+                Text(label)
+                    .style(selectedTab == type ? .button1_onBrand : .button1_Primary)
+                    .frame(width: 108, height: .buttonHeight)
+                    .background(
+                        RoundedRectangle(cornerRadius: .buttonCornerRadius)
+                            .fill(
+                                selectedTab == type
+                                    ? Color.accent.primary : Color.background.secondary
+                            )
+                    )
+            }
+        }
+        .buttonStyle(.plain)
+        .pointerStyle(.link)
+    }
+}
+
+// MARK: - Task Card
+struct TaskCard: View {
+    var item: TaskItem? = nil
+    var automation: SavedAutomationModel? = nil
+    @State private var isHovered = false
+    
+    var body: some View {
+        VStack(alignment: .leading) {
+            Text(item?.title ?? automation?.name ?? "")
+                .style(.body1_primary)
+            
+            Spacer()
+            
+            HStack {
+                if let application = item?.taskAppplication {
+                    ForEach(application) { app in
+                        app.icon
+                            .resizable()
+                            .scaledToFit()
+                            .frame(width: 16, height: 16)
+                    }
+                }
+                
+                Spacer()
+                
+                if let totalRun = automation?.totalRuns {
+                    Text("Runs: \(totalRun)")
+                        .style(.captionSmall_primary)
+                        .padding(.vertical, 5)
+                        .padding(.horizontal, 8)
+                        .background(Color.background.tertiary)
+                        .cornerRadius(4)
+                }
+            }
+        }
+        .padding(.cardInternalPaddingLarge)
+        .frame(width: 280, height: 120)
+        .background(
+            RoundedRectangle(cornerRadius: 12)
+                .fill(
+                    isHovered ? Color.background.secondary.opacity(0.6) : Color.background.secondary
+                )
+        )
+        .onHover { hovering in
+            isHovered = hovering
+            if hovering {
+                NSCursor.pointingHand.push()
+            } else {
+                NSCursor.pop()
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+// MARK: - Tab Enum
+enum TabType: String, CaseIterable, Identifiable {
+    case suggestions = "Suggestions"
+    case pinned = "Pinned"
+    
+    var id: String { rawValue }
+}

+            id: uuidV5(from: prompt),
+            name: prompt,
+            automation: updatedPlan,
+            createdAt: Date(),
+            lastModified: Date(),

+    func uuidV5(from name: String,
+                namespace: UUID = UUID(uuidString: "6ba7b811-9dad-11d1-80b4-00c04fd430c8")!) -> UUID {
+
+        let namespaceBytes = withUnsafeBytes(of: namespace.uuid) { Array($0) }
+        let nameBytes = Array(name.utf8)
+
+        // Combine
+        var data = Data()
+        data.append(contentsOf: namespaceBytes) // now valid
+        data.append(contentsOf: nameBytes)
+
+        // SHA1
+        let sha1 = Insecure.SHA1.hash(data: data)
+        var uuidBytes = Array(sha1.prefix(16))
+
+        uuidBytes[6] = (uuidBytes[6] & 0x0F) | 0x50
+        uuidBytes[8] = (uuidBytes[8] & 0x3F) | 0x80
+
+        // Convert [UInt8]  UUID
+        return uuidBytes.withUnsafeBytes {
+            UUID(uuid: $0.load(as: uuid_t.self))
         }
     }
